<user_name>Pedro Melgarejo<//user_name><Date>1571369457182< /Date><pics>None<//pics><user_id>113883210970581253033</user_id><rating>1<//rating>< Review>
We are giving this restaurant a 1 star due to costumer service. My family and I walked in after soccer practice to enjoy a family dinner. We were seated quickly which started off great, but it took a very long time to have our order placed. We were about to walk out and leave but decided to give it a try. But as the night went on, I regret staying.The food was good. A 7 out of 10. When it came to pay, my wife and I were questioning our bill, because the price appeared to be too high for what we had ordered. When asked for the ticket they brought the original receipt with prices. My wife and I added up the total with our calculator on our phone and the math was not correct. We were OVER charged by 12.00. When we respectfully brought our concern to the waitress on duty, She immediatly got defensive and immediately blamed the other waitress who had left. My wife and I did not come off as aggressive or upset we just wanted to make sure we were charged appropriately. We even told her, (because she seemed way more upset than we did, mind you we were the ones over charged) we weren't trying to blame her, we just wanted to make sure it was done correctly. We waited for an apology but instead she walked to the back where the kitchen was. She then came back and rang us up at the correct price. That was the end of our dinner. No sorrys, no thank you for coming in, no have a good night as all customer service industries thrive on. The customer and their experiences at their business is ehat makes the buisness thrive and customers coming back. But because of poor customer service we will not be returning. We hope no one else has the same experience  my wife and young children had on October 17th, 2019.< /Review>

<review>I've been going here for a few years, and have never been disappointed.
Sandwiched in between a nail salon and vacuum store, I didn't originally feel like this was very well placed, but being in a strip mall I guess that's not always a choice.
I always go for the sushi, but have tried numerous other items on the menu. Yesterday was exceptionally busy as we went during the lunch hour and Paradise Sushi is clearly a favorite for an afternoon break.
In spite of the hustle and bustle, we were greeted and seated mediately. Our waitress was prompt, friendly, and always efficient. Food was delivered within a reasonable amount of time & looked like art on a plate.
Parking can be a challenge during the lunch hour, but its a huge parking lot so there's always something - just might be a bit of a trek...
Highly recommend!<//review>< Pics>

<Name>Ryan Milani</Name><Time>1480191820845<//Time><Rate>4</Rate>< text>
Not the best sushi I've had, but it's a pretty great all-you-can-eat option in a convenient location. They have a Santa Rosa location for a little better atmosphere. It gets busy on the weekends, so prepare for a wait if you go during those peak times. It's a no frills small room with minimal decorations so not the most beautiful place to eat, but hey...All you can eat! The lunch price is slightly less expensive then dinner. So I like to go early and miss the crowds and eat for less. Walk it off after with a easy stroll over the bridge and you're in downtown Petaluma.</text>

Ordered the black tonkotsu ramen, which had a very rich broth, perfect amount of garlic flavor, and well prepared chashu. The service was very attentive, with food arriving promptly. < review>
I noticed some people gave this place one star some people gave his place to Stars well I guess I understand everybody has their own taste and their own likes and dislikes so I'm going to just give you mine. I for one eat at many many ramen restaurants and I do mean many LOL now my experience it was nothing but glorious if you will. I was greeted kindly upon entering the police have plenty of seating and the kitchen was in Clearview. The place was extremely clean for those of you that like clean eating establishments. And the staff was very attentive and kind. Now for the most important part in my opinion is the food and let me tell you I had the chicken ramen and it was absolutely delicious I would only have one minor complaint and that's that the broth wasn't hot enough in my opinion but that's very minor considering the taste of the broth and the well doneness of the noodles they were al dente with great flavor and texture. Now the most important thing would I come here again absolutely and I plan on bringing my family and friends the next time I visit this fine establishment. So if I were you I would definitely give this place a try I honestly don't think you would get disappointed but then again some people have been here and have only rated it one star but in my opinion even they should give this place a second try. Hope you give them a chance and let me know what you think.< /review>

He claimed that our bird was calcium-deficient and that's why it lost the nail. That we should feed it Calcium. That the nail "should" grow back eventually.

The bird was in a state of shock and distressed because it was hurt. < Review>
Expert troubleshooting, quick leak detection, and superior service just when we needed it most.   It‚Äôs not every day that you see a professional go the extra mile and opt for a more difficult procedure for them in order to save a homeowner money and get the job done as quickly as possible.

Joe Arnold visited our home right on time. He asked me a few questions, took a look at the water damaged area, and said that the job would require a plumber to crawl under my house; Joe was by himself and is not a young man. He said that it would be better if he could call out another of their plumbers, because he would also need a second set of hands to assist with the job.  After trying to call for backup, he told me that it might take a day or two before he could tackle the job. I explained how not being able to use our sinks, toilets or showers for 24+ hours already had been a huge problem for our busy family of 4 (2 teens included).  Joe said that he was a father of three and that he totally understood. He offered to start immediately if I would be willing to be his second set of hands up top, while he crawled around underneath the house.  Joe let me know when to open the faucets, turn the water supply off and back on again, and walked me through shooting some compressed air down the damaged hot water pipe to dry it out so he could re-solder the damaged pipe.
Joe far exceeded my expectations and prevented a lot of extra mess, expense and delays by opting to take the more difficult route of crawling under the house instead of just cutting right into my living room wall.
I highly recommend Joe and Bill Metzger plumbing to anyone‚Ä¶ They‚Äôre now my new go-to Plumber.</Review>
